ChatGPT: 

Ja — Claude Code-inputtet er **meget stærkt**, og jeg er enig i hovedretningen. Det hjælper især med at skære igennem alt det, der ellers kunne blive til scope-creep.

Min vurdering: **vi skal ikke “løse HOLD” ved at begynde at ændre reward/action space/EDL/HDP nu.** Vi skal først gøre HOLD-problemet målbart og adskille fire mulige kilder:

```text
1. Config contamination
2. Greedy q50 policy attractor
3. Action-mask → HOLD fallback
4. Svag Q-value separation mellem actions
```

Claude siger reelt det samme: clean baseline først, ingen 50k endnu, ingen HDP/EDL-performance endnu, og May 22-runs skal være debug/confounded evidence, ikke final evidence. Det matcher også den reproducibility-infrastruktur vi allerede har bygget: manifest, verifier, `.env` cleanup og run registry. 

## Det vigtigste jeg tager fra Claude

### 1. `epsilon_eval=0.0` skal eksplicit ind

Det er en god pointe. Lige nu er det sandsynligvis default/preset, men det skal ikke være implicit. For thesis-baseline skal vi tydeligt sige:

```text
Training: epsilon-greedy exploration
Evaluation: pure greedy policy, epsilon_eval = 0.0
```

Så clean manifest bør eksplicit have:

```json
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_EPSILON_EVAL": "0.0"
```

og `expected_iqn_config` bør have:

```json
"epsilon_eval": 0.0
```

Claude anbefaler også `eval_interval=2000`, fordi 5000 kun giver 5 datapunkter på en 25k læringskurve. Det er jeg enig i. Hvis du vil vise “learning/convergence”, er 5 punkter for lidt. Med 2000 får du ca. 12–13 eval-punkter, hvilket er meget bedre til plots. 

### 2. Action mask kan være en skjult HOLD-generator

Det her er nok den vigtigste nye diagnosticeringspointe.

Hvis en action bliver blocked og miljøet fallbacker til HOLD, så kan HOLD opstå af to forskellige årsager:

```text
A. IQN valgte selv HOLD
B. IQN valgte BUY/SELL/REBALANCE, men masken blokerede, og effective action blev HOLD
```

Det er kæmpe forskel.

Hvis vi ikke logger det, kan vi fejlagtigt tro at IQN “lærer HOLD”, selvom miljøet ofte omskriver agentens ønskede action til HOLD. Claude siger derfor, at vi bør logge/aggregere `action_was_masked` eller masked-action-rate. Det er jeg helt enig i. 

### 3. HOLD-problemet skal vurderes med tre tal efter clean run

Efter clean baseline skal vi ikke bare kigge på return. Vi skal kigge på:

```text
1. Collapse rate:
   hvor mange seeds ender med HOLD% > 90%?

2. Masked-action-rate:
   hvor ofte bliver requested action ændret til HOLD?

3. Q-value spread:
   hvor stor er forskellen mellem bedste og næstbedste action?
```

Hvis Q-spread er meget lille, så er argmax måske næsten tilfældig/tie-breaking. Hvis Q-spread er stor og HOLD vinder, så er HOLD en reel learned preference. Hvis masked-rate er høj, så er det environment/action-mask-problemet. Det er en meget præcis diagnoseplan.

### 4. V1-visualiseringerne bør porteres — men ikke før clean baseline er i gang

Claude peger på noget vigtigt: V1 havde bedre thesis-facing visualiseringer end V2 lige nu. Især:

```text
compute_action_estimates()
visualize_iqn_decision_distribution.py
plot_last_day_quantile_functions
plot_last_day_scores
summary dashboard
algorithmic baselines
```

Det er meget relevant, fordi de kan vise IQN som **distributional RL**, ikke bare som en sort boks med final return. Claude fremhæver især `visualize_iqn_decision_distribution.py` som en stærk figur: quantile function per action, return-distribution, risk-adjusted score og q10/q25/q50/q75/q90/CVaR-table. 

Men rækkefølgen er vigtig: først clean baseline i gang/afklaret, så port visualiseringer.

## Hvad jeg ikke er helt enig i / vil justere

Claude nævner et tidspunkt “fire toggle-runs” med IQN-only/IQN+HDP/IQN+EDL/IQN+HDP+EDL, men korrigerer senere sig selv: HDP og EDL er post-processing/enrichment oven på IQN audit, ikke nødvendigvis fire nye træninger. Den korrigerede version er den rigtige:

```text
Én IQN-training
→ IQN audit
→ HDP post-processing
→ EDL post-processing
→ thesis/demo dashboard
```

Det er vigtigt, for ellers spilder vi tid på unødvendige træninger. Claude siger også selv senere, at IQN-training og demo/thesis track er to forskellige spor: manifest-pipelinen producerer artifacts, mens demo/notebook/presentation-laget læser precomputed artifacts og genererer figurer. 

## Min anbefalede vej nu

Vi skal gøre HOLD-problemet endeligt diagnosticerbart før clean run.

Ikke en stor rewrite. Kun en lille patch + manifest update.

### Step 1 — patch manifest

I `configs/experiments/clean_25k_baseline_v1.json`:

```json
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_EPSILON_EVAL": "0.0",
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_LEARNING_CURVE_EVAL_INTERVAL": "2000"
```

og i expected config:

```json
"epsilon_eval": 0.0
```

Hvis `eval_interval` ikke er en del af `IQNConfig`, skal den ikke nødvendigvis i `expected_iqn_config`; den skal bare verificeres som experiment/runtime setting, ikke model hyperparameter.

### Step 2 — patch logging, ikke behavior

Tilføj kun diagnostic logging. Ikke ændre action-mask behavior.

Vi skal have følgende i training/eval artifacts:

```text
requested_action
effective_action
action_was_masked
epsilon
action_selection_mode = random/greedy/eval_greedy
q_value_spread = best_score - second_best_score
best_action
second_best_action
```

Minimum er:

```text
action_was_masked
requested_action
effective_action
epsilon
```

Det ændrer ikke træningssemantik. Det gør kun diagnosen mulig.

### Step 3 — kør clean_25k_baseline_v1

Når verifier passer, kør kun:

```powershell
$env:PYTHONPATH = "src"
python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.verify_experiment_config --config configs/experiments/clean_25k_baseline_v1.json
python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.run_iqn_experiment_from_config --config configs/experiments/clean_25k_baseline_v1.json
```

Det er allerede dokumenteret som exact planned final-evidence candidate. 

### Step 4 — post-run diagnosis

Efter run skal vi lave én summary:

```text
seed
final_return
final_sharpe
total_trades
HOLD%
BUY%
SELL%
REBALANCE%
masked_action_rate
mean_q_spread
collapse_status
```

Så kan vi endeligt sige:

```text
HOLD skyldes primært learned greedy policy
eller
HOLD skyldes action-mask fallback
eller
HOLD skyldes low Q-spread/tie-like argmax
eller
HOLD er reduceret efter clean config
```

```text
   - effective_action
   - action_was_masked
   - epsilon

4. Aggregate per seed summary if possible:
   - masked_action_rate
   - requested_action_counts
   - effective_action_counts
   - HOLD%
   - BUY%
   - SELL%
   - REBALANCE%
   - mean_q_value_spread if available

5. Do not alter training semantics.
   If any diagnostic requires invasive code changes, skip it and report why.

6. Run:
   python -m py_compile on all modified Python files.
   python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.verify_experiment_config --config configs/experiments/clean_25k_baseline_v1.json

7. Stop.
   Do not run training.

Report:
- files modified
- exact manifest changes
- whether eval_interval=2000 is supported
- whether epsilon_eval is now verified
- what diagnostic columns are now logged
- py_compile status
- config verifier status
```


## 1. Ret `iqn.eval_interval`

Nuværende:

```json
"eval_interval": 5000,
```

Ret til:

```json
"eval_interval": 2000,
```

Hvorfor: `5000` giver kun ca. 5 eval-punkter på 25k steps. `2000` giver ca. 12–13 punkter, som er meget bedre til learning/convergence plots.

## 2. Ret env override for eval interval

Nuværende:

```json
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_LEARNING_CURVE_EVAL_INTERVAL": "5000",
```

Ret til:

```json
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_LEARNING_CURVE_EVAL_INTERVAL": "2000",
```

## 3. Tilføj epsilon eval i `iqn`

I din `"iqn"`-blok har du:

```json
"epsilon_start": 1.0,
"epsilon_final": 0.05,
"epsilon_decay_steps": 15000,
```

Ret til:

```json
"epsilon_start": 1.0,
"epsilon_final": 0.05,
"epsilon_eval": 0.0,
"epsilon_decay_steps": 15000,
```

## 4. Tilføj epsilon eval i `env_overrides`


tilføj:

Så blokken bliver:

```json
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_EPSILON_START": "1.0",
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_EPSILON_FINAL": "0.05",
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_EPSILON_EVAL": "0.0",
"STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_IQN_EPSILON_DECAY_STEPS": "15000",
```

## 5. Tilføj epsilon eval i `expected_iqn_config`

```json
"epsilon_final": 0.05,
```

tilføj:


## Hvorfor ikke mere?

Jeg ville **ikke** ændre tickers, datoer, seeds, score mode, LayerNorm, batch size, replay capacity, tau samples eller target update nu.

Det her manifest er netop din **rene baseline**. Den skal ikke tunes mere lige nu. Den skal kun gøres bedre til diagnosticering og plots.

Efter ændringen bør du køre:

```powershell
$env:PYTHONPATH="src"
python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.verify_experiment_config --config configs/experiments/clean_25k_baseline_v1.json
```

Hvis verifieren fejler på `epsilon_eval`, betyder det sandsynligvis bare, at `verify_experiment_config.py` endnu ikke checker det felt. Så skal verifieren udvides til også at assert’e `epsilon_eval`. Det bør den gøre, fordi vi nu vil have eval-protokollen eksplicit.

# The Guldmand Detailed Roadmap for IQN v3.6

## Current status headline

- Project moved from demo_2 smoke tests to demo_5 thesis-evidence pipeline.
- Mode A verifies live market data acquisition without hidden import fallback.
- Mode B supports reproducible thesis experiments using frozen FinRL-generated import/master data.
- Demo_5 IQN single-seed is complete.
- Demo_5 IQN multiseed is complete, but original q50_minus_cvar setup showed no-trade instability in 3/5 seeds.
- HOLD-collapse/no-trade diagnostic is complete.
- Main root cause was Q-value instability caused by raw FinRL state scale, especially cash around 1,000,000.
- LayerNorm has been implemented as the IQN state-encoder stabilization fix.
- q50 LayerNorm variants are useful as stable diagnostic/thesis evidence.
- CVaR-penalty calibration remains a model-quality issue.
- Hierarchical DSS policy PoC is implemented.
- Combined IQN + HierarchicalDecisionPolicy audit is implemented.
- EDL-C teacher-imitation gate is implemented as integration evidence only.
- EDL-C should not be treated as proof of better market correctness or trading performance.
- Correct EDL methodology has been clarified from the EDL paper/repo.
- EDL-A hindsight-supervised learning is now the main correctness/performance uncertainty track.
- Counterfactual EDL-A hindsight oracle is the current active work item.
- Next after counterfactual oracle: EDL-A dataset builder, reference-aligned EDL training, and IQN/HDP/EDL ablation tests.
- Web PoC and report writing should begin after the technical roadmap reaches a stable evidence package.

## FinRL data pipeline ✅

- FinRL YahooDownloader chunked ✅
- yfinance browser-session fallback ✅ / firefox135
- CSV import fallback ✅ / only when explicitly allowed
- canonical cache ✅
- cache-origin metadata ✅
- data completeness validation ✅
- row count by ticker ✅
- failed ticker reporting ✅
- missing ticker reporting ✅
- download attempts metadata ✅
- final source metadata ✅
- Mode A / Mode B separation ✅
- Reproducible frozen import/master file for Mode B ✅

- Mode A is diagnostic/acquisition mode ✅
- Mode B is main experiment mode ✅

ChatGPT:

Ikke:

`-u` betyder unbuffered output, så du får mere live output i notebooken.

## Hvor lang tid tager den?

Mit bedste estimat:

```text
10 seeds × ca. 4–8 minutter per seed
= ca. 40–80 minutter totalt
```

Måske lidt længere, hvis eval hvert `2000` steps gør den mærkbart tungere end før. Så realistisk:

```text
45–90 minutter
```

Det er et multiseed-run med:

```text
10 seeds
25,000 training steps per seed
eval checkpoints ca. hver 2,000 steps
demo10_new / 10 tickers
LayerNorm + q50
```

Så det er ikke en “smoke test” længere. Det er et rigtigt clean baseline-run.

## Logger den til W&B?

`run_iqn_experiment_from_config.py` logger ikke selv til W&B. Den gør kun dette:

```text
1. loader manifest
2. rydder IQN env vars
3. sætter env_overrides
4. kører verify
5. delegater til multiseed launcher
```

Det står også direkte i filen: scriptet indeholder ingen training logic selv, men kalder `run_iqn_learning_curve_multiseed_launcher.main()` som execution backend. 

Så svaret er:

```text
W&B logging afhænger af launcher/smoke-test runner og dine W&B env/settings.
```

Hvis W&B er enabled i dit setup, så ja, sandsynligvis. Hvis W&B er disabled/offline eller mangler API key, så nej eller offline/local.

Før du kører, kan du hurtigt tjekke:

```python
import os
for key in ["WANDB_MODE", "WANDB_PROJECT", "WANDB_ENTITY", "WANDB_API_KEY"]:
    print(key, "=", "***" if key == "WANDB_API_KEY" and os.environ.get(key) else os.environ.get(key))
```

Hvis du vil undgå W&B for dette run:

```python
import os
os.environ["WANDB_MODE"] = "disabled"
```

Men jeg ville **ikke disable W&B**, hvis formålet er thesis evidence og du allerede har styr på at W&B-filer nu ryger i run folders. Det er faktisk nyttigt at have tracking på clean baseline.

ChatGPT:

Ja, du kan godt loade både `.env` og `.env.wandb.local` i notebooken — **men gør det kontrolleret**.

Min anbefaling er:

```text
1. Load .env først, men uden override
2. Load .env.wandb.local bagefter, kun WANDB_* keys
3. Lad clean_25k_baseline_v1.json styre IQN-hyperparametre
```

Det er sikkert, fordi `run_iqn_experiment_from_config.py` alligevel rydder IQN-hyperparameter env vars og sætter dem fra manifestet, før den kører verify/training. Men W&B-vars bliver ikke ryddet, så dem kan du fint sætte fra `.env.wandb.local`.

Sæt denne setup-celle øverst i notebooken:

```python
from pathlib import Path
import os
import sys

REPO_ROOT = Path.cwd()

assert (REPO_ROOT / "src" / "stock_investment_dss").exists(), (
    f"Notebook must be run from repo root. Current cwd: {REPO_ROOT}"
)

os.environ["PYTHONPATH"] = "src"


def load_env_file(path, *, override=False, allowed_prefixes=None):
    path = Path(path)
    if not path.exists():
        print(f"Skipped missing env file: {path}")
        return

    loaded = 0

    for raw_line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
        line = raw_line.strip()

        if not line or line.startswith("#") or "=" not in line:
            continue

        key, value = line.split("=", 1)
        key = key.strip()
        value = value.strip().strip('"').strip("'")

        if allowed_prefixes is not None:
            if not any(key.startswith(prefix) for prefix in allowed_prefixes):
                continue

        if override or key not in os.environ:
            os.environ[key] = value
            loaded += 1

    print(f"Loaded {loaded} values from {path}")


# Load general project env safely.
# This should NOT be used as the source of truth for IQN hyperparameters.
load_env_file(".env", override=False)

# Load W&B credentials/settings.
# Only WANDB_* keys are accepted from this file.
load_env_file(".env.wandb.local", override=True, allowed_prefixes=("WANDB_",))

print("Repo root:", REPO_ROOT)
print("Python:", sys.executable)
print("PYTHONPATH:", os.environ.get("PYTHONPATH"))

for key in ["WANDB_MODE", "WANDB_PROJECT", "WANDB_ENTITY", "WANDB_API_KEY"]:
    value = os.environ.get(key)
    if key == "WANDB_API_KEY" and value:
        value = "***"
    print(f"{key} =", value)
```

Hvis du vil sikre online W&B logging, skal output gerne vise noget ala:

```text
WANDB_MODE = online
WANDB_PROJECT = ...
WANDB_ENTITY = ...
WANDB_API_KEY = ***
```

Hvis `WANDB_MODE` stadig er `None`, men `WANDB_API_KEY` findes, kan W&B ofte stadig logge online. Men jeg ville være eksplicit i `.env.wandb.local`:

```env
WANDB_MODE=online
WANDB_PROJECT=din_project_name
WANDB_ENTITY=din_personlige_eller_team_entity
WANDB_API_KEY=...
```

Derfor loader den kun:

men den ignorerer disse, fordi de **ikke** starter med `WANDB_`:

## Løsning 1 — behold dine nuværende variable og map dem til W&B

Tilføj dette efter din env-loader-celle:

```python
import os

# Map project-specific W&B env vars to standard W&B env vars
if os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT"):
    os.environ["WANDB_PROJECT"] = os.environ["STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT"]

if os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENTITY"):
    os.environ["WANDB_ENTITY"] = os.environ["STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENTITY"]

if os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENABLED", "").lower() == "true":
    os.environ["WANDB_MODE"] = "online"

for key in ["WANDB_MODE", "WANDB_PROJECT", "WANDB_ENTITY", "WANDB_API_KEY"]:
    value = os.environ.get(key)
    if key == "WANDB_API_KEY" and value:
        value = "***"
    print(f"{key} =", value)
```

Men så skal din loader også tillade `STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_` fra `.env.wandb.local`:

```python
load_env_file(
    ".env.wandb.local",
    override=True,
    allowed_prefixes=("WANDB_", "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_"),
)
```

## Løsning 2 — nemmest: tilføj standard W&B-variabler direkte

I `.env.wandb.local`, skriv også:

```env
WANDB_MODE="online"
WANDB_PROJECT="StockInvestmentDSS"
WANDB_ENTITY="guldmand-SDU"
WANDB_API_KEY="KEY"
```

Så behøver du ikke mapping.

Du kan stadig beholde dine egne:

```env
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENABLED="true"
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT="StockInvestmentDSS"
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENTITY="guldmand-SDU"
```

men standard W&B-library kigger typisk efter `WANDB_PROJECT`, `WANDB_ENTITY`, `WANDB_MODE`, `WANDB_API_KEY`.

## Jeg ville gøre dette nu

Opdater loader-kaldet til:

```python
load_env_file(
    ".env.wandb.local",
    override=True,
    allowed_prefixes=("WANDB_", "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_"),
)
```

og tilføj mapping-blokken bagefter.

Når det virker, bør du se:

```text
WANDB_MODE = online
WANDB_PROJECT = StockInvestmentDSS
WANDB_ENTITY = guldmand-SDU
WANDB_API_KEY = ***
```

Så kan du køre `verify` igen og derefter clean baseline.

Hvis den API-key du indsatte i chatten var en rigtig nøgle og ikke placeholder, så rotér den i W&B bagefter.

Brug i stedet denne setup-celle:

```python
from pathlib import Path
import os
import sys

REPO_ROOT = Path.cwd()

assert (REPO_ROOT / "src" / "stock_investment_dss").exists(), (
    f"Notebook must be run from repo root. Current cwd: {REPO_ROOT}"
)

# Required for `python -m stock_investment_dss...`
os.environ["PYTHONPATH"] = "src"


def load_env_file(path, *, override=False, allowed_prefixes=None):
    path = Path(path)

    if not path.exists():
        print(f"Skipped missing env file: {path}")
        return

    loaded = 0

    for raw_line in path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
        line = raw_line.strip()

        if not line or line.startswith("#") or "=" not in line:
            continue

        key, value = line.split("=", 1)
        key = key.strip()
        value = value.strip().strip('"').strip("'")

        if allowed_prefixes is not None:
            if not any(key.startswith(prefix) for prefix in allowed_prefixes):
                continue

        if override or key not in os.environ:
            os.environ[key] = value
            loaded += 1

    print(f"Loaded {loaded} values from {path}")


# Load general project env safely.
# IMPORTANT:
# This is not the source of truth for IQN hyperparameters.
# The clean experiment manifest controls IQN config.
load_env_file(".env", override=False)

# Load W&B-related settings.
# We allow both:
# - standard WANDB_* keys
# - project-specific STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_* keys
#
# IMPORTANT:
# We do NOT force WANDB_MODE=online here.
# The existing project/run logic should decide how W&B is initialized.
load_env_file(
    ".env.wandb.local",
    override=True,
    allowed_prefixes=("WANDB_", "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_"),
)

print("Repo root:", REPO_ROOT)
print("Python:", sys.executable)
print("PYTHONPATH:", os.environ.get("PYTHONPATH"))

for key in [
    "WANDB_MODE",
    "WANDB_PROJECT",
    "WANDB_ENTITY",
    "WANDB_API_KEY",
    "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENABLED",
    "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT",
    "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENTITY",
]:
    value = os.environ.get(key)
    if key == "WANDB_API_KEY" and value:
        value = "***"
    print(f"{key} =", value)
```

Med din `.env.wandb.local` bør du så få cirka:

```text
Loaded 4 values from .env.wandb.local
Repo root: c:\Users\gurug\Dropbox\DataScience\Speciale\D-IQN-DSS\FinRL_IQN
```

## Tjek det før du kører

Kør denne fra repo-roden:

```powershell
Select-String -Path .\src\stock_investment_dss\**\*.py `
  -Pattern "wandb.init|WANDB_DIR|run_paths.run_directory|run_directory" `
  -SimpleMatch:$false |
  Select-Object Path, LineNumber, Line
```

Du leder efter noget i stil med:

```python
wandb.init(
    ...
    dir=str(run_paths.run_directory),
    ...
)
```

Hvis du ser det, er vi gode.

## Ekstra sikkerhed i notebooken

Jeg ville **ikke** sætte `WANDB_MODE=online`, men du kan godt sætte en debug-print før run:

```python
import os

for key in [
    "WANDB_DIR",
    "WANDB_MODE",
    "WANDB_PROJECT",
    "WANDB_ENTITY",
    "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENABLED",
    "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT",
    "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENTITY",
]:
    print(key, "=", os.environ.get(key))
```

Jeg ville ikke manuelt sætte `WANDB_DIR`, medmindre vi opdager at koden ikke bruger `dir=str(run_paths.run_directory)`. Din eksisterende run-logik bør helst styre placeringen.

## Tjek efter første seed starter

Når runnet er begyndt og første seed har oprettet en run folder, kan du i en anden terminal køre:

```powershell
# Tjek om root-wandb er kommet tilbage
Test-Path .\wandb

# Find nyeste W&B mapper under outputs/runs
Get-ChildItem .\outputs\runs -Recurse -Directory -Filter "wandb" |
  Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending |
  Select-Object -First 10 FullName, LastWriteTime
```

Det ønskede resultat er:

```text
Test-Path .\wandb
False
```

og W&B-mapper under:

```text
outputs\runs\<run_id>\wandb
```

## Hvis `.\wandb` dukker op igen

Så stop ikke nødvendigvis hele træningen straks, men notér det. Det betyder bare, at W&B init ikke får en per-run `dir`. Så skal vi bagefter patche `wandb.init(..., dir=str(run_paths.run_directory))`.

Min vurdering: hvis Copilot-patchen om W&B-dir stadig er i `run_iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test.py`, så bør du ikke få root `wandb/` igen.

## Hvad med de andre to filer?

`wandb_tracking.py` har også en `wandb.init(...)`, men den sætter **ikke** `dir=...`. Den bruger dine projekt-specifikke env vars:

```python
project = os.getenv("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT", "stock-investment-dss")
entity = os.getenv("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENTITY") or None
mode = os.getenv("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_MODE") or None
```

og kalder derefter `wandb.init(...)` uden `dir`. Hvis den fil blev brugt aktivt i et run, kunne den potentielt lave root `wandb/` igen. Men dit clean IQN learning-curve run ser ud til at bruge den lokale `init_optional_wandb_run(...)` i `run_iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test.py`, hvor `dir` er sat korrekt. 

`experiment_tracking.py` er også en generisk/ældre tracker med `wandb.init(...)` uden `dir`, men den ligger under `src/stockdss/...`, ikke den nuværende `src/stock_investment_dss/...` struktur. Den ser derfor ikke ud til at være den relevante kodevej for clean baseline-runnet.

ChatGPT:

Ja — det er faktisk en rigtig god idé.

Lav en **separat notebook-celle** før det store IQN-run, som tester:

```text
Python kernel ✅
torch ✅
wandb import ✅
W&B credentials ✅
W&B project/entity ✅
W&B local files under outputs/runs/... ✅
basic metric logging ✅
artifact/log finish ✅
```

Brug denne celle:

```python
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
import os
import sys

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.optim as optim

try:
    import wandb
except ImportError as exc:
    raise RuntimeError("wandb is not installed in this conda env.") from exc


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# W&B smoke-test run folder
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y_%m_%d_%H%M%S")
run_dir = Path("outputs") / "runs" / f"{timestamp}_wandb_relu_smoke_test"
run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

project = os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT", "StockInvestmentDSS")
entity = os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENTITY") or None
enabled = os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENABLED", "").lower() == "true"

print("Python:", sys.executable)
print("Torch:", torch.__version__)
print("W&B enabled:", enabled)
print("W&B project:", project)
print("W&B entity:", entity)
print("Run dir:", run_dir.resolve())
print("WANDB_API_KEY:", "***" if os.environ.get("WANDB_API_KEY") else None)

if not enabled:
    raise RuntimeError("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENABLED is not true.")

if not os.environ.get("WANDB_API_KEY"):
    raise RuntimeError("WANDB_API_KEY is missing.")


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Tiny ReLU network smoke test
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

torch.manual_seed(42)

x = torch.randn(256, 10)
true_w = torch.randn(10, 1)
y = x @ true_w + 0.1 * torch.randn(256, 1)

model = nn.Sequential(
    nn.Linear(10, 32),
    nn.ReLU(),
    nn.Linear(32, 1),
)

optimizer = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=1e-3)
loss_fn = nn.MSELoss()


wandb_run = wandb.init(
    project=project,
    entity=entity,
    name=f"wandb_relu_smoke_test_{timestamp}",
    group="wandb-smoke-tests",
    job_type="relu_smoke_test",
    config={
        "test_type": "5_epoch_relu_nn",
        "epochs": 5,
        "optimizer": "Adam",
        "lr": 1e-3,
        "loss": "MSELoss",
        "input_dim": 10,
        "hidden_dim": 32,
        "output_dim": 1,
        "run_dir": str(run_dir.resolve()),
    },
    dir=str(run_dir),
    tags=["wandb-smoke-test", "relu", "not-thesis-result"],
)

for epoch in range(1, 6):
    optimizer.zero_grad()
    pred = model(x)
    loss = loss_fn(pred, y)
    loss.backward()
    optimizer.step()

    loss_value = float(loss.item())
    print(f"Epoch {epoch}/5 - loss={loss_value:.6f}")

    wandb_run.log(
        {
            "epoch": epoch,
            "train/loss": loss_value,
        },
        step=epoch,
    )

wandb_run.finish()

print("\nDone.")
print("Expected local W&B folder under:")
print(run_dir.resolve())
print("\nCheck root wandb folder should ideally be False:")
print("Root ./wandb exists:", Path("wandb").exists())
```

Når den er færdig, skal du gerne se:

```text
Epoch 1/5 - loss=...
...
Epoch 5/5 - loss=...
Done.
Root ./wandb exists: False
```

Og du bør kunne finde W&B-filer her:

```text
outputs/runs/<timestamp>_wandb_relu_smoke_test/wandb/
```

Hvis `Root ./wandb exists: True`, så stop lige før det store run — så skal vi fikse W&B-dir-håndtering først.

Hvis den logger korrekt til W&B-web og samtidig placerer local W&B-filer under `outputs/runs/...`, så kan du trygt gå videre til:

```python
!python -u -m stock_investment_dss.runner.run_iqn_experiment_from_config --config configs/experiments/clean_25k_baseline_v1.json
```

## Endnu bedre minimal variant

Hvis du vil undgå at gøre runneren for specifik permanent, kan du gøre det env-styret:

```python
job_type = (
    get_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_JOB_TYPE",
        default="iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test",
    )
    or "iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test"
)

tags_text = (
    get_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_TAGS",
        default="iqn,learning-curve,distributional-rl,stockdss",
    )
    or "iqn,learning-curve,distributional-rl,stockdss"
)

tags = [tag.strip() for tag in tags_text.split(",") if tag.strip()]
```

og så:

```python
run = wandb.init(
    project=project,
    entity=entity or None,
    name=run_paths.run_id,
    group=group,
    job_type=job_type,
    config=config,
    dir=str(run_paths.run_directory),
    tags=tags,
)
```

Så kan du sætte i `.env.wandb.local`:

```env
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_JOB_TYPE="iqn_hold_diagnostic"
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_TAGS="iqn,hold-diagnostic,clean-25k,q50,layernorm,distributional-rl,stockdss"
```

Det er den pæneste løsning, fordi samme runner senere kan bruges til andre typer runs uden at være hardcoded som HOLD-diagnostic.

## Hvad jeg ville gøre lige nu

```text
src/stock_investment_dss/runner/run_iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test.py
```

## Endnu bedre, men stadig lille: gør det env-styret

Hvis du ikke vil hardcode runneren som HOLD-diagnostic permanent, så ret til:

```python
job_type = (
    get_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_JOB_TYPE",
        default="iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test",
    )
    or "iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test"
)

tags_text = (
    get_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_TAGS",
        default="iqn,learning-curve,distributional-rl,stockdss",
    )
    or "iqn,learning-curve,distributional-rl,stockdss"
)

tags = [tag.strip() for tag in tags_text.split(",") if tag.strip()]

run = wandb.init(
    project=project,
    entity=entity or None,
    name=run_paths.run_id,
    group=group,
    job_type=job_type,
    config=config,
    dir=str(run_paths.run_directory),
    tags=tags,
)
```

Så kan du sætte i `.env.wandb.local`:

```env
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_JOB_TYPE="iqn_hold_diagnostic"
STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_TAGS="iqn,hold-diagnostic,clean-25k,q50,layernorm,distributional-rl,stockdss"
```

Det er den bedste løsning, fordi:

```text
relu smoke-testen forbliver relu_smoke_test
clean_25k bliver iqn_hold_diagnostic
fremtidige runs kan få andre tags uden at ændre kode
```

## Vigtigt

`run_iqn_experiment_from_config.py` er kun adapteren. Den loader manifest, rydder IQN-env-vars, verifierer og delegerer til multiseed launcher; den indeholder ikke selv W&B-metadata. 

Så W&B-job_type/tags skal rettes dér, hvor `wandb.init(...)` faktisk kaldes i IQN-runneren — altså `run_iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test.py`.

Min anbefaling: vælg **env-styret løsning** nu. Then run:

```powershell
python -m py_compile src/stock_investment_dss/runner/run_iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test.py
python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.verify_experiment_config --config configs/experiments/clean_25k_baseline_v1.json
```

Derefter kan du køre ReLU smoke-testen og bagefter clean baseline uden at W&B-tags blandes sammen.

from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
import os
import sys

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.optim as optim

try:
    import wandb
except ImportError as exc:
    raise RuntimeError("wandb is not installed in this conda env.") from exc


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# W&B smoke-test run folder
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y_%m_%d_%H%M%S")
run_dir = Path("outputs") / "runs" / f"{timestamp}_wandb_relu_smoke_test"
run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

project = os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_PROJECT", "StockInvestmentDSS")
entity = os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENTITY") or None
enabled = os.environ.get("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENABLED", "").lower() == "true"

print("Python:", sys.executable)
print("Torch:", torch.__version__)
print("W&B enabled:", enabled)
print("W&B project:", project)
print("W&B entity:", entity)
print("Run dir:", run_dir.resolve())
print("WANDB_API_KEY:", "***" if os.environ.get("WANDB_API_KEY") else None)

if not enabled:
    raise RuntimeError("STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_ENABLED is not true.")

if not os.environ.get("WANDB_API_KEY"):
    raise RuntimeError("WANDB_API_KEY is missing.")


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------
# Tiny ReLU network smoke test
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------

torch.manual_seed(42)

x = torch.randn(256, 10)
true_w = torch.randn(10, 1)
y = x @ true_w + 0.1 * torch.randn(256, 1)

model = nn.Sequential(
    nn.Linear(10, 32),
    nn.ReLU(),
    nn.Linear(32, 1),
)

optimizer = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=1e-3)
loss_fn = nn.MSELoss()


wandb_run = wandb.init(
    project=project,
    entity=entity,
    name=f"wandb_relu_smoke_test_{timestamp}",
    group="wandb-smoke-tests",
    job_type="relu_smoke_test",
    config={
        "test_type": "5_epoch_relu_nn",
        "epochs": 5,
        "optimizer": "Adam",
        "lr": 1e-3,
        "loss": "MSELoss",
        "input_dim": 10,
        "hidden_dim": 32,
        "output_dim": 1,
        "run_dir": str(run_dir.resolve()),
    },
    dir=str(run_dir),
    tags=["wandb-smoke-test", "relu", "not-thesis-result"],
)

for epoch in range(1, 6):
    optimizer.zero_grad()
    pred = model(x)
    loss = loss_fn(pred, y)
    loss.backward()
    optimizer.step()

    loss_value = float(loss.item())
    print(f"Epoch {epoch}/5 - loss={loss_value:.6f}")

    wandb_run.log(
        {
            "epoch": epoch,
            "train/loss": loss_value,
        },
        step=epoch,
    )

wandb_run.finish()

print("\nDone.")
print("Expected local W&B folder under:")
print(run_dir.resolve())
print("\nCheck root wandb folder should ideally be False:")
print("Root ./wandb exists:", Path("wandb").exists())

starter en **ny Python-proces**, og den proces kalder sin egen `wandb.init(...)` inde i `run_iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test.py`. Adapteren `run_iqn_experiment_from_config.py` gør kun env setup + verify og delegerer videre; den har ikke selv W&B-logik.

## Adapter med W&B override flags?

Ja, det kunne faktisk være en god forbedring senere.

`run_iqn_experiment_from_config.py` kunne få flags som:

```powershell
--wandb-job-type iqn_hold_diagnostic
--wandb-tags iqn,hold-diagnostic,clean-25k,q50,layernorm,distributional-rl,stockdss
--wandb-group clean-25k-hold-diagnostic
```

og så sætte env vars før den kalder launcheren:

```python
if args.wandb_job_type:
    os.environ["STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_JOB_TYPE"] = args.wandb_job_type

if args.wandb_tags:
    os.environ["STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_TAGS"] = args.wandb_tags

if args.wandb_group:
    os.environ["STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_GROUP"] = args.wandb_group
```

Men for at det virker, skal `init_optional_wandb_run(...)` i `run_iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test.py` også læse de env vars. Lige nu læser den allerede `STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_GROUP`, men `job_type` og `tags` er hardcoded.

Så den fulde forbedring ville være:

```python
job_type = (
    get_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_JOB_TYPE",
        default="iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test",
    )
    or "iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test"
)

tags_text = (
    get_environment_variable(
        "STOCK_INVESTMENT_DSS_WANDB_TAGS",
        default="iqn,learning-curve,distributional-rl,stockdss",
    )
    or "iqn,learning-curve,distributional-rl,stockdss"
)

tags = [tag.strip() for tag in tags_text.split(",") if tag.strip()]
```

og så:

```python
run = wandb.init(
    project=project,
    entity=entity or None,
    name=run_paths.run_id,
    group=group,
    job_type=job_type,
    config=config,
    dir=str(run_paths.run_directory),
    tags=tags,
)
```

Det er pænt, men det er en lille kodeændring.

ChatGPT:


Så processen er ikke død. Notebook-outputtet er bare ikke særligt informativt lige nu.

Det skyldes sandsynligvis en kombination af:

```text
!python -u giver live stdout,
men selve runneren logger primært via logger/log-filer og W&B
```

Derfor kan notebook-cellen godt se “stille” ud, selvom træningen kører.

## Gør dette i en ny terminal mens cellen kører

Fra repo-roden:

```powershell
cd "C:\Users\gurug\Dropbox\DataScience\Speciale\D-IQN-DSS\FinRL_IQN"

Get-ChildItem .\outputs\runs -Directory |
  Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending |
  Select-Object -First 5 Name, LastWriteTime
```

Find den nyeste run-folder. Derefter:

```powershell
$latest = Get-ChildItem .\outputs\runs -Directory |
  Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending |
  Select-Object -First 1

$latest.FullName
Get-ChildItem $latest.FullName -Recurse -File |
  Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending |
  Select-Object -First 20 FullName, LastWriteTime
```

Hvis der ligger en logfil under fx:

```text
outputs\runs\<run_id>\logs\run.log
```

så kan du følge den sådan her:

```powershell
Get-Content "$($latest.FullName)\logs\run.log" -Wait -Tail 50
```

## Tjek om root wandb kom tilbage

Kør også:

```powershell
Test-Path .\wandb
```

Hvis den siger:

```text
False
```

så er W&B stadig korrekt placeret under run-folderen.

Tjek W&B under outputs:

```powershell
Get-ChildItem .\outputs\runs -Recurse -Directory -Filter "wandb" |
  Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending |
  Select-Object -First 10 FullName, LastWriteTime
```

## Om “smoke test” navnet

Ja, det er irriterende at run-navnet/job_type stadig siger `iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test`, men det er **ikke ReLU-smoke-testen**. Det er bare den historiske runner-fil/job_type. W&B-graferne viser tydeligt IQN-training metrics, ikke ReLU-testen.

Så lige nu: **lad den køre**.

## Hvornår skal du blive bekymret?

Bliv først bekymret hvis:

```text
W&B holder op med at opdatere i mange minutter
CPU/GPU/Python-processen forsvinder
outputs/runs/<latest>/ ikke får nye filer
notebook-cellen stopper med returncode/error
```

Ellers er det bare et langt run.

Når første seed er færdig, bør du begynde at se flere output-filer under `outputs/runs`, og senere en multiseed-summary-run/mappe.

Kæmpe milepæl. Det vigtige først:

```text
✅ clean_25k_baseline_v1 kørte færdig
✅ config verification PASS — 17/17
✅ 10/10 seeds completed successfully
✅ multiseed summary completed successfully
✅ total runtime ca. 41 minutter
```

Nu er næste step **ikke** mere training. Nu skal vi analysere outputtet og HOLD-diagnosticeringen.

## 1. Find run-mapperne

Kør først i PowerShell fra repo-roden:

```powershell
$base = "C:\Users\gurug\Dropbox\DataScience\Speciale\D-IQN-DSS\FinRL_IQN\outputs\runs"

Get-ChildItem $base -Directory |
  Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending |
  Select-Object -First 20 Name, LastWriteTime
```

Du skal især finde:

```text
2026_05_23_082851_d_iqn_dss_iqn_learning_curve_multiseed_launcher
```

og sandsynligvis en ny:

```text
..._d_iqn_dss_iqn_learning_curve_multiseed_summary
```

plus 10 seed-run-mapper.

## 2. Se den vigtigste multiseed summary

Prøv:

```powershell
$base = "C:\Users\gurug\Dropbox\DataScience\Speciale\D-IQN-DSS\FinRL_IQN\outputs\runs"

$latestSummary = Get-ChildItem $base -Directory |
  Where-Object { $_.Name -match "multiseed_summary" } |
  Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending |
  Select-Object -First 1

$latestSummary.FullName

Get-ChildItem $latestSummary.FullName -Recurse -File |
  Select-Object FullName, Length |
  Format-Table -AutoSize
```

Derefter kig på final records CSV:

```powershell
Get-Content "$($latestSummary.FullName)\summary\iqn_learning_curve_multiseed_final_records.csv"
```

Det bør give os seed-level resultaterne: return, Sharpe, trades, drawdown osv.

## 3. Se HOLD-diagnostic summary

Fordi Copilot patchen tilføjede HOLD-diagnostic fields, skal vi nu tjekke om de faktisk findes:

```powershell
Get-ChildItem $base -Recurse -File -Filter "hold_diagnostic_summary.json" |
  Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending |
  Select-Object -First 20 FullName, LastWriteTime
```

Hvis de findes, kan du samle dem sådan her:

```powershell
$holdFiles = Get-ChildItem $base -Recurse -File -Filter "hold_diagnostic_summary.json" |
  Sort-Object FullName

$rows = foreach ($file in $holdFiles) {
    $json = Get-Content $file.FullName -Raw | ConvertFrom-Json

    [pscustomobject]@{
        File = $file.FullName
        masked_to_hold_count = $json.masked_to_hold_count
        masked_action_rate = $json.masked_action_rate
        hold_pct_requested = $json.hold_pct_requested
        hold_pct_effective = $json.hold_pct_effective
    }
}

$rows | Format-Table -AutoSize
```

Det her er det centrale for HOLD-problematikken.

## 4. Kør Q-value spread diagnostic

Nu skal vi bruge det nye post-run script på seed-runs. Først find seed-run-mapperne fra dette launcher-run:

```powershell
$base = "C:\Users\gurug\Dropbox\DataScience\Speciale\D-IQN-DSS\FinRL_IQN\outputs\runs"

Get-ChildItem $base -Directory |
  Where-Object { $_.Name -match "iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test" -and $_.LastWriteTime -gt [datetime]"2026-05-23 08:20" } |
  Sort-Object Name |
  Select-Object Name, LastWriteTime
```

Så kan du køre Q-spread diagnostic for hver seed:

```powershell
$seedRuns = Get-ChildItem $base -Directory |
  Where-Object { $_.Name -match "iqn_learning_curve_smoke_test" -and $_.LastWriteTime -gt [datetime]"2026-05-23 08:20" } |
  Sort-Object Name

foreach ($run in $seedRuns) {
    Write-Host "Running Q-spread diagnostic for $($run.Name)"
    python -m stock_investment_dss.runner.run_hold_qvalue_spread_diagnostic --run-dir $run.FullName
}
```

Det burde skrive:

```text
hold_qvalue_spread_diagnostic.csv
```

i hver run-mappe.

## 5. Det vi skal afgøre nu

Når du har final records + HOLD summaries, kan vi konkludere på Claudes tre forklaringer:

```text
A) IQN requested HOLD directly
   → hold_pct_requested høj

B) Mask/action fallback ændrede BUY/SELL/REBALANCE til HOLD
   → masked_action_rate høj
   → masked_to_hold_count høj

C) Weak Q-value separation / policy attractor
   → Q-spread lav eller HOLD vinder konsekvent med lille margin
```

Hvis `hold_pct_requested` og `hold_pct_effective` begge er lave/moderate, og trades > 0 for de fleste seeds, så er clean baseline langt bedre end de confounded May 22-runs.

## 6. Send mig helst disse outputs

Send først denne:

```powershell
Get-Content "$($latestSummary.FullName)\summary\iqn_learning_curve_multiseed_final_records.csv"
```

og derefter HOLD-tabellen fra:

```powershell
$rows | Format-Table -AutoSize
```

Så kan jeg hjælpe med at lave den endelige clean HOLD-diagnose:

```text
config contamination fixed?
collapse rate?
masked action fallback?
learned HOLD attractor?
Q-spread issue?
```

Lige nu er status: **training-runnet lykkedes. Nu starter selve diagnosen.**

ChatGPT:

Det her er faktisk **meget stærkt resultat** for HOLD-diagnosen.

## Kort konklusion

Clean 25k-runnet viser:

```text
✅ Config contamination er væk
✅ 10/10 seeds gennemført
✅ action mask fallback er IKKE årsagen
✅ masked_to_hold_count = 0 for alle seeds
✅ masked_action_rate = 0.00 for alle seeds
✅ kun 1/10 seeds er ren HOLD/no-trade collapse
✅ 9/10 seeds handler faktisk
```

Det vigtigste diagnostiske fund er dette:

```text
masked_action_rate = 0.00
masked_to_hold_count = 0
```

for alle 10 seeds. Det betyder: **HOLD kommer ikke fra action-mask fallback**. Altså ikke:

```text
IQN vælger BUY/SELL
→ mask blokerer
→ env laver fallback til HOLD
```

Det sker ikke her. HOLD er derfor primært en **policy/Q-value preference**, ikke en mask-bug. 

## Seed-resultaterne siger noget vigtigt

Ud fra `iqn_learning_curve_multiseed_final_records.csv`:

```text
Seed 1:  +1.21%, 37 trades
Seed 2: +42.69%, 506 trades
Seed 3: +36.34%, 5 trades
Seed 4: +12.84%, 2 trades
Seed 5: +81.98%, 567 trades
Seed 6:   0.00%, 0 trades  ← true HOLD collapse
Seed 7: +110.79%, 10 trades
Seed 8: +110.83%, 9 trades
Seed 9: +80.62%, 8 trades
Seed 10: +1.79%, 80 trades
```

Så collapse-rate er:

```text
1 / 10 seeds = 10%
```

Det er **meget bedre** end de gamle demo_5/May-runs, hvor du havde 3/5 no-trade seeds i nogle setups.

## Hvad Q-spread siger

Q-spread diagnosticen viser også, at der faktisk er Q-separation i flere seeds.

Eksempler:

```text
Seed 5: final mean spread ≈ 1.18
Seed 4: final mean spread ≈ 0.41
Seed 7: final mean spread ≈ 0.39
Seed 1: final mean spread ≈ 0.26
Seed 10: final mean spread ≈ 0.13
Seed 3: final mean spread ≈ 0.04
```

Det betyder: nogle seeds har tydelig policy-separation, mens andre stadig har svagere separation. Seed 6 er stadig vigtig at undersøge, fordi den endte i `{'HOLD': 600}` og 0 trades.

Men samlet er diagnosen nu:

```text
HOLD problem is reduced, not eliminated.
It is not caused by action-mask fallback.
It is residual seed-dependent IQN policy/Q-value attractor behavior.
```

Det er præcis den type konklusion Claude lagde op til.

## Vigtig nuance

CSV’en siger:

```text
score_mode = q50
risk_lambda = 0.75
```

Når `score_mode=q50`, bør `risk_lambda` være irrelevant for action scoring. Den står bare med som config/legacy-felt. Det er ikke nødvendigvis et problem, men i rapport/summary ville jeg skrive:

```text
The run used q50 action scoring. The risk_lambda field is logged but inactive under q50 scoring.
```

Så ingen læser det som om CVaR-penalty stadig var aktiv.

## Næste skridt

Nu skal du ikke køre mere training endnu. Nu skal du lave én clean summary-fil.

Bed Copilot om at lave:

```text
outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_hold_diagnostic_summary.md
outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_hold_diagnostic_metrics.csv
```

med:

```text
seed
return
sharpe
max_drawdown
total_trades
final_cash_weight
action_counts
masked_action_rate
masked_to_hold_count
hold_pct_requested
hold_pct_effective
q_spread_mean
q_spread_final
collapse_status
```

Konklusionen i den fil bør være:

```text
- Clean 25k baseline completed successfully.
- Config verifier passed 17/17.
- 10/10 seeds completed.
- 1/10 seeds showed full HOLD/no-trade collapse.
- 9/10 seeds produced non-zero trading activity.
- action-mask fallback is ruled out as primary HOLD cause because masked_action_rate=0 across all seeds.
- Remaining HOLD behavior is consistent with seed-dependent Q-policy attractor / weak action-value separation.
- LayerNorm + clean manifest substantially reduced but did not fully eliminate HOLD collapse.
- This is promising PoC evidence, not production trading-strategy evidence.
```

## Mini-konklusion til TODO/rapportnoter

Du kan skrive:

```text
Clean 25k IQN-only HOLD diagnostic completed. The run used a manifest-verified configuration with LayerNorm, q50 scoring, 25k steps, epsilon_eval=0.0, and 10 seeds. All seeds completed successfully. The action-mask fallback hypothesis was rejected: masked_to_hold_count=0 and masked_action_rate=0.00 for all seeds. Only one seed showed full HOLD/no-trade collapse, while the remaining nine seeds traded. The remaining HOLD behavior is therefore best interpreted as seed-dependent Q-policy attractor behavior rather than an environment mask bug.
```

Det her er et meget bedre og mere thesis-sikkert resultat end før.


```text

4. What remains unresolved
```


# Clean 25k HOLD Diagnostic — Plot Summary

Generated: 2026-05-23 15:12:38

Experiment: `clean_25k_baseline_v1` — 10 seeds, 25,000 training steps, score_mode=q50, LayerNorm=true
Source artifacts: May 23 2026 08:28–09:09 UTC+2 clean run.
**No training was performed to generate these plots.**

## Key findings (from plots)

- **masked_action_rate = 0.0 for all seeds** (plot 3): action-mask fallback is ruled out as the cause of HOLD behavior.
- **Seed 6** is the only full HOLD/no-trade collapse (plots 1, 2, 10).
- Q-value spread is non-zero across all seeds (plot 4), ruling out pure random tie-breaking.
- Spread varies substantially between seeds (seed 5: mean=0.61; seed 9: mean=0.11).
- Seed 6 has moderate spread (mean=0.15) yet fully collapsed — HOLD collapse is non-linear.
- Epsilon schedule is identical across seeds and decays to 0.05 by step ~15,000 (plot 9).
- The remaining HOLD issue is seed-dependent Q-policy attractor / weak action-value separation.

## Plots

### seed_level_total_return.png
Bar chart of final eval total return by seed. Seed 6 highlighted as collapsed.

### seed_level_total_trades.png
Bar chart of total trades by seed. Seed 6 = 0 trades.

### masked_action_rate.png
Masked action rate per seed — 0.0 across all seeds, ruling out action-mask fallback.

### q_value_spread_mean_and_final.png
Grouped bar comparing q_spread_mean and q_spread_final per seed.

### requested_vs_effective_action_distribution.png
Stacked 100% bar of training action distribution per seed. Requested = effective (masked_action_rate=0).

### eval_return_learning_curve_mean_std.png
Mean ± 1 std eval total return over training checkpoints.

### eval_sharpe_learning_curve_mean_std.png
Mean ± 1 std annualized Sharpe over training checkpoints.

### iqn_loss_curve_mean_std.png
Mean ± 1 std IQN loss in 500-step bins across 10 seeds.

### epsilon_curve.png
Epsilon decay curve (seed 1 representative; identical across all seeds).

### seed6_vs_seed7_vs_seed8_comparison.png
2×2 multi-panel: Q-spread, eval return, action distribution, and loss for seeds 6, 7, 8.

ChatGPT:

Yes — I have enough information. Below is my proposed `outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_hold_diagnostic_interpretation.md`.

It is based on the clean 25k summary, the plot summary, and the reviewed diagnostic evidence: 10/10 seeds completed, seed 6 was the only full no-trade collapse, `masked_action_rate = 0.0` across all seeds, and Q-value spread was non-zero across seeds.  

````markdown
# Clean 25k HOLD Diagnostic Interpretation

Generated from the clean 25k IQN-only diagnostic run and its derived plot package.

Source run family:

- Experiment: `clean_25k_baseline_v1`
- Dataset: `demo_10_new_long_2010_2026_hold_collapse_diagnostic_clean25k`
- Universe: `demo_10_new`
- Tickers: `COST, AVGO, LLY, ORCL, CAT, BA, KO, MCD, WMT, PG`
- Train window: `2010-01-01 → 2023-12-31`
- Eval window: `2024-01-01 → 2026-12-31`
- Seeds: `1–10`
- Training steps: `25,000`
- Score mode: `q50`
- LayerNorm: `true`
- HDP: disabled
- EDL: disabled
- FMP live calls: disabled
- Data mode: frozen data only
- Config verification: `PASS 17/17`

Related artifacts:

- `outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_hold_diagnostic_metrics.csv`
- `outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_hold_diagnostic_summary.md`
- `outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_hold_diagnostic_plots/`
- `outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_hold_diagnostic_plots/plot_summary.md`
- `outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_hold_diagnostic_plots/plot_manifest.json`

---

## 1. Purpose of the diagnostic

The purpose of this diagnostic was to isolate the cause of residual HOLD/no-trade behavior in the IQN-based decision-support agent after three major corrections had already been applied:

1. The raw FinRL state-scale issue had been mitigated using LayerNorm in the IQN state encoder.
2. Experiment-defining IQN hyperparameters had been moved out of global `.env` state and into an explicit experiment manifest.
3. The clean manifest was verified before training, ensuring that the run used the intended configuration rather than residual shell or PowerShell environment variables.

The diagnostic was therefore not designed as a final trading-performance benchmark. Its purpose was narrower: to determine whether remaining HOLD behavior was caused by action-mask fallback, configuration contamination, or a residual value-learning/policy-attractor phenomenon.

---

## 2. Summary of observed results

The clean 25k run completed successfully across all 10 seeds. The verifier passed all 17 expected IQN configuration assertions before training, and every seed completed without runtime failure.

The seed-level outcomes were heterogeneous:

- 9 out of 10 seeds produced non-zero trading activity.
- 1 out of 10 seeds showed full HOLD/no-trade collapse.
- Seed 6 was the only full no-trade collapse, with `total_trades = 0` and final return of `0.00%`.
- Several seeds produced high returns with sparse trading, especially seeds 7 and 8, each of which made only 9–10 trades but achieved approximately `+110%` final eval return.
- Other seeds displayed more active behavior, particularly seeds 2 and 5, with 506 and 567 trades respectively.

The resulting collapse rate was therefore:

```text
full HOLD/no-trade collapse rate = 1 / 10 seeds = 10%
````

This is materially better than the earlier confounded May 22 demo10_new diagnostic runs, which showed higher collapse rates under contaminated hyperparameters. Those earlier runs remain useful as debugging evidence, but not as final thesis performance evidence.

---

## 3. Action-mask fallback is ruled out

The most important diagnostic result is that action-mask fallback was not the source of the remaining HOLD behavior.

Across all 10 seeds:

```text
masked_action_rate = 0.0
masked_to_hold_count = 0
```

This means that the agent was not repeatedly requesting BUY, SELL, or REBALANCE actions that were then blocked by the environment and converted into HOLD. In this clean run, requested actions and effective actions were identical for the purpose of the diagnostic.

Therefore, the following causal explanation is rejected:

```text
IQN requests non-HOLD action
→ action mask blocks it
→ environment converts action to HOLD
→ HOLD collapse appears as an environment artifact
```

Instead, remaining HOLD behavior must be interpreted as arising from the learned IQN policy itself.

---

## 4. Q-value spread interpretation

The Q-value spread diagnostic measures the gap between the best-scoring and second-best-scoring actions at evaluation checkpoints. A spread near zero would suggest random tie-breaking or an almost indifferent policy. The clean run did not show this pattern.

Q-value spread was non-zero across all seeds. This indicates that the final greedy policy was not simply choosing HOLD due to random ties between actions.

However, spread magnitude varied substantially by seed. For example:

* Seed 5 had relatively high separation, with mean spread around `0.61` and final spread around `1.18`.
* Seed 9 had weaker separation, with mean spread around `0.11`.
* Seed 6, the collapsed seed, had moderate spread around `0.15`, not the lowest spread in the group.

This is important because it shows that collapse is not explained by a single linear indicator such as “low Q-spread.” Seed 6 did not collapse because the model had no action preference. It collapsed because its learned Q-value ordering still led the greedy policy into HOLD for the full evaluation trajectory.

The stronger interpretation is therefore:

```text
The residual HOLD issue is a seed-dependent Q-policy attractor, not random tie-breaking.
```

---

## 5. Seed 6 interpretation

Seed 6 is the only full no-trade collapse in the clean 25k run.

It is also diagnostically useful because it does not look like a simple logging, masking, or evaluation bug:

* Its action-mask rate is zero.
* Its Q-value spread is non-zero.
* Its training action distribution is not uniquely extreme compared with all other seeds.
* Its collapse occurs at the final greedy evaluation level, where the learned policy selects HOLD throughout the evaluation trajectory.

This suggests that seed 6 reached a policy basin where HOLD became the dominant greedy action across the encountered evaluation states.

The comparison with seeds 7 and 8 is particularly informative. Seeds 7 and 8 also produced sparse trading policies, but they did not fully collapse. Instead, they made a small number of high-impact trades and then held positions through the evaluation window. This indicates that sparse trading alone should not be treated as failure. The failure mode is specifically the complete absence of trading activity, not merely a low trading frequency.

Thus, the distinction should be:

```text
Sparse high-conviction policy: few trades, non-zero position taking, positive portfolio effect.
Full HOLD/no-trade collapse: no trades, no portfolio exposure change, zero return.
```

Seed 6 belongs to the second category.

---

## 6. Learning-curve interpretation

The evaluation return and Sharpe learning curves provide useful but non-classical evidence of learning.

The evaluation return curve increases substantially during early and mid training, but it does not form a smooth monotonic convergence curve. Instead, it shows high seed variance and some decline after the peak. This is expected in a financial RL setting where policy quality is sensitive to random initialization, market regime exposure, and the interaction between exploration and greedy evaluation.

The Sharpe curve is more stable than the return curve, but still shows seed-level variability. Seed 6 is excluded or null in Sharpe calculations where no trades make the metric undefined.

The IQN loss curve should be interpreted carefully. It does not show classical monotonic convergence. In fact, the loss increases over training. This does not automatically invalidate the learned policies, because distributional value-learning loss in a non-stationary financial environment is not equivalent to final trading performance. However, it does mean that the thesis should avoid claiming that the IQN loss itself converges in the classical supervised-learning sense.

A thesis-safe interpretation is:

```text
The learning curves show policy-level improvement and non-trivial learned behavior across most seeds, but not classical monotonic convergence of the IQN training loss. Therefore, performance and policy diagnostics are interpreted jointly rather than using loss convergence as the sole evidence of learning.
```

---

## 7. Epsilon schedule interpretation

The epsilon schedule is deterministic and identical across all 10 seeds:

* `epsilon_start = 1.0`
* `epsilon_final = 0.05`
* `epsilon_decay_steps = 15000`

This means that exploration decays to its final value by approximately step 15,000, leaving the remaining part of training to consolidate the learned policy under low exploration.

The clean run used greedy evaluation with:

```text
epsilon_eval = 0.0
```

This is appropriate for a clean baseline because it evaluates the learned deterministic policy. However, it also makes residual attractor behavior visible. If a seed has learned a HOLD-dominant Q-value ordering, greedy evaluation will expose that directly.

This should be treated as a feature of the diagnostic, not as a bug:

```text
The use of epsilon_eval=0.0 makes the final greedy policy observable. It is therefore suitable for diagnosing whether the agent has truly learned a trading policy or has converged to a HOLD attractor.
```

Future ablations may test non-zero evaluation epsilon or alternative exploration schedules, but such ablations should be reported as separate model-quality experiments, not retroactively mixed with the clean baseline.

---

## 8. What is ruled out

The clean diagnostic rules out the following explanations as primary causes of the remaining HOLD issue:

### 8.1 Configuration contamination

The run was manifest-driven and passed the expected IQN configuration verifier before training. This distinguishes the clean 25k result from earlier May 22 runs affected by residual environment variables.

### 8.2 Action-mask fallback

The masked action rate was zero across all seeds. The environment did not force requested non-HOLD actions into HOLD.

### 8.3 Pure random tie-breaking

Q-value spread was non-zero across all seeds. The final policies were not simply selecting actions from numerically identical Q-values.

### 8.4 Lack of any learning signal

Nine out of ten seeds traded, and several produced substantial positive returns. This indicates that the system is capable of learning non-trivial policies under the clean configuration.

---

## 9. What remains unresolved

The clean diagnostic does not prove that the IQN agent is a robust trading strategy. It shows that the main previously suspected confounders have been isolated and that the remaining HOLD problem is narrower and more interpretable.

The remaining unresolved issue is:

```text
seed-dependent Q-policy attractor robustness
```

In practical terms, this means that different random seeds can still converge to materially different greedy policies under the same data, architecture, and hyperparameters. Some seeds learn active or sparse high-conviction trading behavior, while one seed converges to a full no-trade HOLD policy.

This is a model-quality and robustness issue, not an environment-mask bug.

Potential future explanations include:

* insufficient robustness of the value-learning optimization landscape,
* sensitivity to random initialization,
* limited ability of q50 scoring to separate active from passive policies in trending markets,
* interaction between transaction costs, sparse rewards, and greedy evaluation,
* insufficient incentive to escape the HOLD attractor once the policy has entered it.

These should be treated as future ablation targets, not as unresolved implementation errors.

---

## 10. Thesis-safe interpretation

The clean 25k diagnostic supports the following thesis-safe interpretation:

> After earlier experiments revealed a potential HOLD/no-trade collapse problem, a clean manifest-driven IQN baseline was introduced to eliminate configuration contamination and isolate the source of the behavior. The clean run verified the intended configuration before training and completed 10 independent seeds. Only one seed showed full no-trade collapse, while nine seeds produced non-zero trading activity. Since the masked action rate was zero across all seeds, action-mask fallback is ruled out as the primary cause. The remaining HOLD behavior is therefore best interpreted as a seed-dependent Q-policy attractor: under greedy q50 evaluation, some independently trained IQN policies converge to a state-action value ordering in which HOLD dominates across the evaluation trajectory. LayerNorm and clean hyperparameter control substantially reduce, but do not fully eliminate, this failure mode.

This interpretation is academically stronger than claiming that the HOLD issue is “solved.” The correct conclusion is:

```text
The HOLD problem has been isolated and reduced, not eliminated.
```

---

## 11. What should not be claimed

The following claims should be avoided:

* Do not claim that the IQN agent is a production-ready trading strategy.
* Do not claim that the IQN loss curve shows classical convergence.
* Do not claim that LayerNorm fully solves HOLD collapse.
* Do not claim that the clean 25k run proves robustness across market regimes.
* Do not use the confounded May 22 25k/50k runs as headline performance evidence.
* Do not claim that sparse trading is automatically a failure; distinguish sparse high-conviction trading from full no-trade collapse.
* Do not claim that EDL or HDP improves trading performance based on this IQN-only diagnostic.

---

## 12. Recommended next steps

The immediate next step is to preserve this clean diagnostic as the current reference point.

Recommended actions:

1. Commit or archive the clean 25k metrics, summary, plots, and manifest.
2. Update `TODO.md` so that:

   * clean HOLD diagnostic instrumentation is marked complete,
   * clean 25k IQN-only baseline is marked complete,
   * clean 25k HOLD diagnosis is marked complete,
   * clean diagnostic plots are marked complete,
   * this interpretation note becomes the current thesis-evidence artifact.
3. Use this diagnostic in the thesis as evidence of methodological correction and controlled failure-mode analysis.
4. Only after this evidence is saved should further ablations be considered.

Potential later ablations:

* clean 50k rerun under the verified manifest,
* epsilon schedule ablation,
* non-zero evaluation epsilon ablation,
* reward/action incentive ablation,
* q50 versus risk-sensitive score-mode ablation,
* IQN-only versus IQN + HDP comparison,
* IQN + HDP + EDL-A uncertainty gate after EDL-A has been validated.

These should not be mixed into the clean 25k baseline. They should be documented as separate experiments.

---

## 13. Final conclusion

The clean 25k HOLD diagnostic provides a controlled and thesis-safe baseline for interpreting the IQN agent.

The main conclusion is:

```text
In the cleaned D-IQN-DSS setup, HOLD/no-trade collapse is no longer primarily explained by configuration contamination or action-mask fallback. Under the verified q50 + LayerNorm configuration, 9/10 seeds produced non-zero trading activity and 1/10 seeds fully collapsed to HOLD. The remaining failure mode is best understood as a seed-dependent Q-policy attractor / weak action-value separation phenomenon. This is a meaningful diagnostic finding for a point-in-time decision-support thesis, but it is not evidence of a production-ready trading strategy.
```

## Problem: “configuration contamination was the primary cause”

I README’en står der ifølge outputtet:

```text
Configuration contamination was the primary cause of earlier HOLD collapse.
```

Det er lidt for stærkt.

Den rigtige thesis-safe formulering er:

```text
Configuration contamination was a major confounder and likely substantial contributor to earlier HOLD collapse.
```

Hvorfor? Fordi clean 25k ikke kun ændrede én ting. Du havde også LayerNorm, clean manifest, q50, verified config, og den nye 25k diagnostic setup. Vi kan derfor stærkt sige:

```text
config contamination made earlier runs invalid as final evidence
```

men ikke 100% isoleret bevise:

```text
config contamination alone was the primary cause
```

Det matcher også v2-notens mere forsigtige tone: action-mask fallback ruled out, residual issue remains a seed-dependent Q-policy attractor, and HOLD is reduced but not eliminated.

```text
Goal:
Make the evidence package more thesis-safe by removing overclaims.

Required wording fixes:

1. Replace any claim equivalent to:
   "Configuration contamination was the primary cause of earlier HOLD collapse"
   with:
   "Configuration contamination was a major confounder and likely substantial contributor to earlier HOLD collapse."

2. Replace any claim equivalent to:
   "This proves configuration contamination caused HOLD collapse"
   with:
   "This shows that the earlier May 22 runs were confounded and should not be used as final performance evidence."

3. It is OK to keep:
   - collapse rate changed from 7/10 in the contaminated 50k diagnostic to 1/10 in the clean 25k diagnostic
   - action-mask fallback ruled out in the clean 25k run
   - residual HOLD behavior interpreted as seed-dependent Q-policy attractor
   - LayerNorm + clean manifest substantially reduced but did not eliminate HOLD collapse

4. If the phrase "seven-fold reduction" appears, keep it only if it is phrased descriptively:
   "The observed collapse count decreased from 7/10 in the contaminated 50k diagnostic to 1/10 in the clean 25k run."
   Do not use it to claim strict causal proof.

5. If "optimal training length" or "25k exceeds the optimal training length" appears, soften it to:
   "The observed eval curve suggests that, for this setup, earlier stopping may have produced higher mean eval return. This should be treated as an early-stopping hypothesis, not as a final conclusion."

6. Preserve these final conclusions:
   - 10/10 seeds completed
   - 1/10 full HOLD/no-trade collapse
   - 9/10 seeds active
   - masked_action_rate=0.0 across all seeds
   - action-mask fallback ruled out
   - residual issue is seed-dependent Q-policy attractor / weak action-value separation
   - promising PoC evidence, not production trading-strategy evidence

After patching, print changed lines only.
```

## Hvorfor ikke 50k nu?

Fordi clean 25k allerede viste, at eval return topper tidligere og falder mod 25k. Så 50k kan meget vel bare undersøge “mere greedy lock-in”, ikke forbedre thesis-beviset. Hvis du vil undersøge noget nu, er det smartere at bruge **eksisterende checkpoints** til at diskutere early stopping, fordi du allerede har eval-return curves.

## Mest thesis-økonomiske næste step

Jeg ville gøre dette:

```text
Next thesis evidence decision ⬅️ CURRENT
  - decide whether clean 25k evidence is sufficient for IQN-only baseline
  - decide whether to use existing checkpoint curves for early-stopping discussion
  - decide whether one small ablation is needed
```

## Mere konkret: hvad er næste praktiske step?

Jeg ville ikke starte med “hele thesisen”. Jeg ville starte med én thesis-ready note/section draft:

```text
docs/thesis_sections/clean_25k_iqn_hold_diagnostic_section.md
```

eller hvis du bruger LaTeX:

```text
report/sections/results_clean_25k_hold_diagnostic.tex
```

Den skal være en første version af det, der senere kan indgå i:

```text
Chapter 5 — Results
Chapter 6 — Discussion
```

## Hvad skal den indeholde?

Ikke alt fra evidence package. Kun det thesis-relevante:

```text
1. Why the clean rerun was needed
2. Experimental setup
3. Config verification and reproducibility guard
4. Seed-level results
5. HOLD diagnostic result
6. Action-mask fallback ruled out
7. Q-policy attractor interpretation
8. Learning-curve caveat
9. Limitations
10. Transition to next work / future ablations
```

## Roadmap-mæssigt

Det er derfor, jeg foreslår:

```text
Thesis section drafting ⬅️ CURRENT
```

fordi den forrige fase allerede har produceret:

```text
outputs/run_registry/next_thesis_evidence_decision.md
```

og den note har konkluderet, at næste anbefalede step er at **skrive thesis sections nu**, ikke at køre mere training.

## Hvis du synes “Thesis section drafting” er for bredt

Så kan vi gøre det mere specifikt i roadmap’et:

```text
Clean 25k thesis section draft ⬅️ CURRENT
  - Results subsection draft
  - Discussion subsection draft
  - Methodology/reproducibility paragraph
  - Limitations paragraph
  - figure references and captions
↓
Next experiment decision ⬅️ AFTER SECTION DRAFT
  - decide if one small ablation is still needed
  - otherwise continue thesis writing
```

Jeg synes faktisk denne er bedre og mere præcis end bare “Thesis section drafting”.

## Min anbefalede opdatering

Brug denne i TODO:

```text
Clean 25k thesis section draft ⬅️ CURRENT
  - method/reproducibility paragraph from manifest workflow
  - results subsection from clean 25k evidence package
  - HOLD diagnostic subsection
  - discussion paragraph on residual Q-policy attractor
  - limitations paragraph from caveats package
  - thesis figure references from figure_selection.md
↓
Next experiment decision ⬅️ AFTER SECTION DRAFT
  - only run a small ablation if writing reveals a specific missing claim
  - otherwise continue thesis writing
```

Det er mere kontrolleret: først skriver vi section draft, og **først efter det** vurderer vi om der faktisk mangler et eksperiment.

[18.24.08] Get-Content .\docs\thesis_sections\clean_25k_iqn_hold_diagnostic_section.md -Head 60
# Clean 25k IQN HOLD Diagnostic — Thesis Section Draft

**Experiment:** `clean_25k_baseline_v1`
**Draft date:** 23 May 2026
**Status:** Working note — ready for merge into thesis Chapter 5 (Results) and Chapter 6 (Discussion).
**Source:** `outputs/run_registry/clean_25k_thesis_evidence_package/`

---

## 1. Context and Motivation

Early IQN baseline experiments on the `demo_10_new` universe (May 22, 2026) exhibited a
HOLD/no-trade collapse phenomenon in which the trained agent repeatedly selected the HOLD
action for the entire evaluation trajectory, producing zero trades and zero return. This
behavior was observed in 7 out of 10 seeds in one contaminated 50k-step run and 3 out of 10
seeds in a contaminated 25k-step run.

Subsequent diagnosis revealed that these earlier runs were executed with hyperparameter
settings inherited from residual environment variables (`.env`), which differed from the
intended IQN configuration. Specifically, the contaminated runs used `batch_size=16`,
`replay_capacity=10000`, `target_update_interval=25`, and `num_tau_samples=8` — values
that were not intended for the baseline. These runs are treated as debug/confounded evidence
and must not be used as headline thesis performance evidence.

To obtain a clean, thesis-defensible baseline, a manifest-driven rerun was conducted under
an explicit experiment configuration file (`configs/experiments/clean_25k_baseline_v1.json`)
with a runtime configuration verifier. This section reports the results of that clean run.

---

## 2. Experimental Setup

| Parameter | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| Experiment ID | `clean_25k_baseline_v1` |
| Dataset ID | `demo_10_new_long_2010_2026_hold_collapse_diagnostic_clean25k` |
| Universe | `demo_10_new` |
| Tickers | COST, AVGO, LLY, ORCL, CAT, BA, KO, MCD, WMT, PG |
| Train window | 2010-01-01 → 2023-12-31 |
| Eval window | 2024-01-01 → 2026-12-31 |
| Random seeds | 1 – 10 (10 independent runs) |
| Total training steps | 25,000 |
| Action scoring mode | q50 (median of IQN return distribution) |
| State encoder | LayerNorm (enabled) |
| HDP (Hierarchical Decision Policy) | Disabled |
| EDL (Evidential Deep Learning) | Disabled |
| Live FMP API calls | Disabled (frozen historical data only) |
| Evaluation epsilon | 0.0 (greedy evaluation) |

The evaluation window (2024–2026) corresponds to a predominantly bull-market period for the
`demo_10_new` universe. Results should be interpreted with this regime caveat in mind.

---

## 3. Reproducibility and Manifest Verification

The experiment was executed via a manifest-driven launcher
(`src/stock_investment_dss/runner/run_iqn_experiment_from_config.py`) that reads all
hyperparameters from the experiment manifest JSON and passes them explicitly to the training
pipeline. Prior to training, the runtime configuration verifier
[18.24.09] Get-Content .\docs\thesis_sections\results_clean_25k_hold_diagnostic.tex -Head 80
% ============================================================
% Clean 25k IQN HOLD Diagnostic -- Thesis Section Draft
% Experiment: clean_25k_baseline_v1
% Draft date: 23 May 2026
%
% Intended placement:
%   Chapter 5  (Results)      -- sections 5.1 -- 5.5
%   Chapter 6  (Discussion)   -- sections 6.1 -- 6.2
%
% Do NOT claim:
%   - production-ready trading performance
%   - classical IQN loss convergence
%   - LayerNorm fully solved HOLD collapse
%   - generalisability beyond the demo_10_new universe / bull-market eval regime
% ============================================================

% ---- Main section -------------------------------------------
\section{Clean 25k IQN HOLD Diagnostic}
\label{sec:clean25k_hold_diagnostic}

% ---- 5.1 Context and motivation ----------------------------
\subsection{Context and Motivation}
\label{sec:clean25k_motivation}

Early IQN baseline experiments on the \texttt{demo\_10\_new} universe (May 22, 2026)
exhibited a HOLD/no-trade collapse phenomenon in which the trained agent repeatedly selected
the HOLD action throughout the evaluation trajectory, producing zero trades and zero
portfolio return. In one contaminated 50k-step run, HOLD collapse was observed in 7 out of
10 independent seeds; in a contaminated 25k-step run, in 3 out of 10 seeds.

Subsequent diagnosis established that these earlier runs were executed with hyperparameter
settings inherited from residual environment variables rather than from an explicit
experiment specification. The contaminated runs used \texttt{batch\_size=16},
\texttt{replay\_capacity=10000}, \texttt{target\_update\_interval=25}, and
\texttt{num\_tau\_samples=8}---values that were not intended for the IQN baseline.
These earlier runs are treated as debug/confounded evidence and are not used as headline
thesis performance evidence.

To obtain a clean, reproducible baseline, a manifest-driven rerun was conducted using an
explicit experiment configuration file and a runtime configuration verifier. This section
reports the results of that clean run (\texttt{clean\_25k\_baseline\_v1}).

% ---- 5.2 Experimental setup --------------------------------
\subsection{Experimental Setup}
\label{sec:clean25k_setup}

\begin{table}[ht]
\centering
\caption{Experimental configuration for \texttt{clean\_25k\_baseline\_v1}.}
\label{tab:clean25k_config}
\begin{tabular}{ll}
\hline
\textbf{Parameter} & \textbf{Value} \\
\hline
Experiment ID           & \texttt{clean\_25k\_baseline\_v1} \\
Universe                & \texttt{demo\_10\_new} \\
Tickers                 & COST, AVGO, LLY, ORCL, CAT, BA, KO, MCD, WMT, PG \\
Train window            & 2010-01-01 -- 2023-12-31 \\
Eval window             & 2024-01-01 -- 2026-12-31 \\
Random seeds            & 1 -- 10 (10 independent runs) \\
Total training steps    & 25{,}000 \\
Action scoring mode     & q50 (median of IQN return distribution) \\
State encoder           & LayerNorm (enabled) \\
HDP                     & Disabled \\
EDL                     & Disabled \\
Live FMP API calls      & Disabled (frozen historical data only) \\
Evaluation epsilon      & 0.0 (greedy evaluation) \\
\hline
\end{tabular}
\end{table}

The evaluation window (2024--2026) corresponds to a predominantly bull-market period for
the \texttt{demo\_10\_new} universe. Results are interpreted with this regime caveat in mind.

% ---- 5.3 Reproducibility and manifest verification ---------
\subsection{Reproducibility and Manifest Verification}
\label{sec:clean25k_manifest}

The experiment was executed via a manifest-driven launcher that reads all hyperparameters
from the experiment manifest JSON and passes them explicitly to the training pipeline.

Er det her du mener?

### 6.1 Eval return and Sharpe curves

The mean eval return (averaged over 9 active seeds, excluding the collapsed seed 6) rises
from approximately 32% at training step 0 to a peak of approximately 83% at step 10,000,
then declines to approximately 55% at step 25,000. The standard deviation across seeds is
large throughout training, reflecting genuine inter-seed variance in learned policies.

The Sharpe ratio shows a similar pattern: improving during early and mid training, with
plateau or slight decline after step 10,000.

The observed eval curve suggests that, for this configuration, **earlier stopping may have
produced higher mean eval return**. This should be treated as an early-stopping hypothesis
only, not as a final conclusion. No formal early-stopping criterion was used in this
experiment. Validation-based early stopping or eval-Sharpe plateau detection are identified
as future work.

Hvad siger du at du ville rette det til?
